## **103. Post by `@wolf.girl.technology` on 2026-04-17**

<div class="bsky-card" markdown="1">

<div class="bsky-header" markdown="1">

<img src="https://cdn.bsky.app/img/avatar/plain/did:plc:bmuca5i6atczdbccgzeqwcl4/bafkreibkipreapnfdck3lol5z77nyqkw22wmlpxy7uqxyegjmu46hpz6um" class="bsky-avatar">

<div class="bsky-author-meta" markdown="1">
**PolyWolf** [@wolf.girl.technology](https://bsky.app/profile/did:plc:bmuca5i6atczdbccgzeqwcl4){:target="_blank"}
<br><small>2026-04-17</small>
</div>
</div>

<div class="bsky-content" markdown="1">

I was wondering why atproto PDS OAuth wasn't working for my self-hosted one. Turns out I needed to change my regex redirection to be the following: ^(/xrpc|/oauth|/@atproto|/.well-known/(atproto-did$|oauth-protected-resource$|oauth-authorization-server$))







</div>
